2025-06-01T02:19:32.8828613Z         package, please make sure that 'mypyc.external.googletest.src' is explicitly added
2025-06-01T02:19:32.8828772Z         to the `packages` configuration field.
2025-06-01T02:19:32.8828790Z 
2025-06-01T02:19:32.8829038Z         Alternatively, you can also rely on setuptools' discovery methods
2025-06-01T02:19:32.8829205Z         (for example by using `find_namespace_packages(...)`/`find_namespace:`
2025-06-01T02:19:32.8829299Z         instead of `find_packages(...)`/`find:`).
2025-06-01T02:19:32.8829303Z 
2025-06-01T02:19:32.8829486Z         You can read more about "package discovery" on setuptools documentation page:
2025-06-01T02:19:32.8829491Z 
2025-06-01T02:19:32.8829736Z         - https://setuptools.pypa.io/en/latest/userguide/package_discovery.html
2025-06-01T02:19:32.8829744Z 
2025-06-01T02:19:32.8830055Z         If you don't want 'mypyc.external.googletest.src' to be distributed and are
2025-06-01T02:19:32.8830301Z         already explicitly excluding 'mypyc.external.googletest.src' via
2025-06-01T02:19:32.8830637Z         `find_namespace_packages(...)/find_namespace` or `find_packages(...)/find`,
2025-06-01T02:19:32.8830968Z         you can try to use `exclude_package_data`, or `include-package-data=False` in
2025-06-01T02:19:32.8831263Z         combination with a more fine grained `package-data` configuration.
2025-06-01T02:19:32.8831272Z 
2025-06-01T02:19:32.8831581Z         You can read more about "package data files" on setuptools documentation page:
2025-06-01T02:19:32.8831588Z 
2025-06-01T02:19:32.8832021Z         - https://setuptools.pypa.io/en/latest/userguide/datafiles.html
2025-06-01T02:19:32.8832029Z 
2025-06-01T02:19:32.8832033Z 
2025-06-01T02:19:32.8832200Z         [^1]: For Python, any directory (with suitable naming) can be imported,
2025-06-01T02:19:32.8832313Z               even if it does not contain any `.py` files.
2025-06-01T02:19:32.8832453Z               On the other hand, currently there is no concept of package data
2025-06-01T02:19:32.8832577Z               directory, all directories are treated like packages.
2025-06-01T02:19:32.8832670Z         ********************************************************************************
